Ideas API

Creating a published idea with image

POST api/v1/ideas

Parameters

Name Description
idea[lab_id] The idea of the lab that hosts the idea
idea[author_id] The user id of the user owning the idea
idea[publication_status] Password
idea[title_multiloc] Multi-locale field with the idea title
idea[body_multiloc] Multi-locale field with the idea body
idea[images] Multipart form encoded images
idea[files] Multipart form encoded files

Request

Headers

Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Bearer eyJ0eXAiOiJKV1QiLCJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJleHAiOjE0OTMzMjE0MzEsInN1YiI6ImIxZTU0NDM1LTRiNTktNGVlNy04ZjFhLTI0MTU0ZTcxM2YyZiJ9.MmBaROzbj9V0d52SzlfWUb6Z_A-Ww1mBPMeFvHwAAX4
Host: example.org
Cookie:

Route

POST api/v1/ideas
